        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1358307825" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6353967818442256691"><b>
  <blockquote>8 out of 10</blockquote>
</b><br/><b>Ревью в моем блоге/This review on my blog<br/><a href='http://living-a-thousand-lives.blogspot.ru/2015/11/air-awakens-by-elise-kova.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Living A Thousand Lives</a></b> <i>(please use Chrome/Yandex browser or Android/IOS to see the page; otherwise, spoiler-tags I use to make my post compact may not work)</i><br/> <br/><b>Short-Soundtrack:</b><br/><div>
  <br/>
  <a href='https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=IYVxpDjTnqI' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Dan Gibson – Wind Walker</a><br/><a href='https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LD137cd7Cw0' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sarah Blasko – I Awake</a><br/><a href='https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=FJDBJCauqSU' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Emika – Destiny Killer</a><br/><br/><b>Genre</b>: high-fantasy, YA+ (upper-YA)<br/><b>Stuff</b>: 2 princes, 1 special girl, elemental magic<br/><b>Setting</b>: capital of the Empire <br/><b>Fail</b>: cliches<br/><b>WOW</b>: characters and chemistry<br/><b>POV</b>: 3rd-person, female<br/><b>Love-Geometry</b>: </div></span>
  <span id="freeText6353967818442256691" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>8 out of 10</blockquote>
</b><br /><b>Ревью в моем блоге/This review on my blog<br /><a href="http://living-a-thousand-lives.blogspot.ru/2015/11/air-awakens-by-elise-kova.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Living A Thousand Lives</a></b> <i>(please use Chrome/Yandex browser or Android/IOS to see the page; otherwise, spoiler-tags I use to make my post compact may not work)</i><br /> <br /><b>Short-Soundtrack:</b><br /><div>
  <br />
  <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=IYVxpDjTnqI" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Dan Gibson – Wind Walker</a><br /><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LD137cd7Cw0" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Sarah Blasko – I Awake</a><br /><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=FJDBJCauqSU" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Emika – Destiny Killer</a><br /><br /><b>Genre</b>: high-fantasy, YA+ (upper-YA)<br /><b>Stuff</b>: 2 princes, 1 special girl, elemental magic<br /><b>Setting</b>: capital of the Empire <br /><b>Fail</b>: cliches<br /><b>WOW</b>: characters and chemistry<br /><b>POV</b>: 3rd-person, female<br /><b>Love-Geometry</b>: seeming<br /><br /><b>Quote-Core</b>: <blockquote><i>“I want a place you hardly dare to even whisper. I want the bravery to not only read but to do. I want a man, not a library boy. A man who is tall and witty and knows more about the world than you would ever dare dream.”</i></blockquote><br />Did you love The Grisha Trilogy? You have a chance to get another HEA for alike characters here. Do you like cartoons, something in Avatar style? I think the author is kinda a fan of, ‘cause, you know, the atmosphere. Maybe you are into Morpheus’s verbal seduction tactic? You’ll get it. <br /><br />Some would call <i>Air Awakens</i> a patchwork blanket of clichés. Agreed, at first, it looks like. But this is a normal thing. We live quite the same lives, experience the same things and still we do it differently. What makes common unique? Halftones and nuances. Elise Kova’s debut story flavored with a yummy sauce that makes it very tasty (at least for me).<br /> <br />In <i>Air Awakens</i> we have a world with four corners of the earth. I know this is the same word we live in. But AA’s has magic! Westerners (the Empire, where our characters live, is on the West, btw) have black hair and dark eyes, olive skin and power over flames. They are Firebearers. Southerners are surprisingly pale, ice-blue-eyed and blond. They command water and are Waterrunners. Those who are from North have very dark skin and the same eyes, they are Groundbreakers and you know what it means. Easterners’ skin is tanned and has a yellowish shade; they have curly brown hair and brown eyes. Their Affinity is air, that makes them Windwalkers or rather had been making, ‘cause there wasn’t a soul with such a gift for over a century. BTW, this is not only an elemental kind of magic, if you have such power, but you can also improve it and learn some mental tricks and stuff. Oh, and not everyone has a gift. This is not a common thing. People afraid of sorcerers. <br /><br />Meet our MC Vhalla Yarl, she’s almost 18-year-old Eastern library apprentice, who is eager for knowledge, curious and nice. She’s not a virgin (what a twist!), not a snob, but a bit narrow-minded at the start of the story. But she’ll get better. You’ll see. <br /><br />Meet the older of our male-leads, it’s Aldrik, crown prince and a royal pain. He’s about 24-25, tall, has a good body, shoulder-length raven hair and black eyes. <br /><blockquote><b><i>“Nothing about him was traditionally handsome, and for it all, he was astonishingly striking.”</i></b></blockquote><br />Also, he’s witty, silver-tongued, snarky… hm, maybe Vhalla would describe him better:<br /><blockquote><b><i>“You, my prince,” she sneered in kind. “You are a self-centered, egotistical, self-absorbed, narrow-sighted, vain, self-important,” she felt her anger finally reach its boiling point, “conceited bastard!” Vhalla cried out.”</i></b></blockquote><br />Yeah, something like that. But it’s not that easy. I mean, he is what he seems but, at the same time, he is not. Oh, one more thing. He’s a Firebearer. A sorcerer. <br /><br />Meet the younger prince Baldair. Not a sorcerer, but a thing. Heartbreaker Prince, they called him. And they have their reasons. <br /><blockquote><b><i>“You’re not the first low-born I have invited to lunch.” He leaned back in his chair, food forgotten. “They come in, swoon over my chambers, prattle about the food endlessly, try everything they can to make eyes at me. By the end of it all, they’re belly up and bare on the bed.”</i></b></blockquote><br />He’s always atop, as I see xDDD Baldair’s ear-length hair is golden, as well as his sun-kissed skin. He has blue eyes, a muscular frame, and an attitude. He acts like a lightheaded, not serious, giddy boy and so on, but, like his brother (with whom Baldair has some issues), he's something more than a careless and easily amused man.<br /><br />Aldrik and Baldair are soldiers. Aldrik commands the Black Legion, the little army of sorcerers. Baldair and Emperor himself lead regular warriors. The Empire is at war with North. When one of the brothers is back from the front with a bad injury, Vhalla helps to save his life. The problem is, she thinks it is Baldair on whom she has a girlish crush and that’s why she tries to find a cure so hard, but the man she has saved is Aldrik. And this is not her only problem at all. She has left a trace on papers with notes about an antidote, a magic one. And once the prince finds out that she’s a sorcerer and how rare her Affinity is, he wouldn't let her be. Yes, he wants her power. He wears black. He’s the-Darkling-like. And Titus-like too. Did you hear me? The Darkling and Titus in one body. But when his brother comes home for a great festivity and sees that Aldrik is spending time with a lesser commoner, he starts to act just like Morpheus. Morpheus, right. Seductive seduction with jokes. Here I go crazy about both of them.<br /><br />Two princes. One special girl with a unique power. It could be boring and predictable, but it turned out being intriguing and sexy. The chemistry between characters themselves and between them and me is strong and raw. I care. I worry. I’m in love. BTW, so far we have no love-triangle.<br /><blockquote><b><i>“Prince Baldair was the better of the two princes. He was kind, thoughtful, lighthearted, and simple to understand. But he didn’t have the same wit of his brother. He didn’t possess the same flair with his words nor grace in his step. He couldn’t command a room in the same way. He certainly didn’t have shoulder-length raven hair nor wonderfully pronounced cheekbones.”</i></b></blockquote><br />Vhalla is favoring just one of them. I guess, it’s rather a manipulative-triangle, but I can sense a true one in the future books, and you know what? I don’t mind it at all. I can’t choose one prince right now, so I can’t blame Vhalla if she would feel the same.<br /><br />Vhalla is a good MC. Has her flaws, makes mistakes, but isn't TSTL. She’s not Rembo or Harry Potter, she’s just a girl who loves reading.<br /><blockquote><b><i>“Tell me, Vhalla, have you ever made love to a man?” He closed the distance between them as he spoke. With a single step, the crown prince was painfully close after asking such a question. “Tell me, have you ever pleasured yourself?”&lt;...&gt;“Whatever it was, I doubt it was very good,” he sneered down at her. She wanted to hit him. “I will tell you why it was not. Because, Vhalla, you think and you watch, but you never do. You can read all the books in this library, be wiser than the master himself someday, and then you will die having never really done anything. You will have only ever lived through everyone else’s experiences.”</i></b></blockquote><br />And now she has to act, to live her life and make her own decisions. I’m sure she will become a fighter, she’ll find love, she is destined for greatness. And I would love to go through this path with her. <br /><br /><b>Air Awakens (Пробуждение воздуха):</b><br /><blockquote>— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1358307825" rel="nofollow noopener">Air Awakens (Пробуждение воздуха)</a> #1/5<br />— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1400002098" rel="nofollow noopener">Fire Falling (Влечение огня) </a>#2/5<br />— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1400002226" rel="nofollow noopener">Earth's End (Край земли)</a> #3/5<br />— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1446477012" rel="nofollow noopener">Water's Wrath (Гнев воды)</a> #4/5<br />— Crystal Crowned (Коронованная кристаллами) #5/5<blockquote></blockquote></blockquote>
</div></span>
  <a data-text-id="6353967818442256691" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7P5QbRI0G1inbR75Mu9Jox2VsUoFPOB+y4bHW81FZB+BbgEakCfN7lhmwb2e2Oj4W5ncvF7aVqKPl7qfxagEIA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Z67PCZBss+Zm/Q4sRRUp1iRrlq+u3pKlTh3iQMoA2g4KPp5+En9lUJn20WjpIoiNYmf7WfU4JHkKDJ+Ewu26MQ==')})
  }
//]]>

Lost in a land of twisted magic and fabled creatures, Haven finds herself unprepared, not just for the feelings she develops for Archeron, but for the warring powers raging inside her.   Her rare and forbidden type of magic may be their only hope . . . but mixing light and dark comes with a steep price.   Haven’s soul. <span id="freeTextContainer2343787607038490794">Elise Kova is a USA Today bestselling author. In her past lives, she has graduated from an MBA program, lived in Japan for a bit, and worked for a Fortune 500 technology company. However, she finds herself much happier in her current reincarnation as full-time author. When not writing, she can usually be found playing video games, drawing, watching anime, or talking with readers on social media. S</span>
  <span id="freeText2343787607038490794" style="display:none">Elise Kova is a USA Today bestselling author. In her past lives, she has graduated from an MBA program, lived in Japan for a bit, and worked for a Fortune 500 technology company. However, she finds herself much happier in her current reincarnation as full-time author. When not writing, she can usually be found playing video games, drawing, watching anime, or talking with readers on social media.
